####################### Guaranteed Fusions ###################

%% The 0 condition for row equality means these partitions always give a fusion of the tensor product scheme for any rank 3 scheme.%%

%%  A lattice diagram representation of guaranteed fusions of the rank 9 tensor product scheme is also included in the PDF uploaded. %%

## We start by listing the Generalised Hamming scheme (GHS) which is one of the guaranteed fusions of the tensor product scheme.

6=8 [ 0 ]

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%% Partitions ruled out using Bannai-Muzychuk Row and Rank condition%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

## The rank of the following fusions is higher than the number of distinct rows. 
##These can be ruled out regardless of the row equality conditions listed in the code output.
## More information and examples on the Bannai-Muzychuk is given in our previously published article and my PhD thesis.

%%%%%%%%%%% Type I Examples %%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

2=7 [ r^2*s-r*s^2-2*r^2+2*r*s-2*r+2*s, l*s^2+r*s^2-3*l*s-2*r*s+l-2*s+1, l*r-2*l*s-r*s+2*l+r+2, l*s+r*s+k-2*l-2*r-2 ]
3=4 [ r^2*s-r*s^2-2*r*s+2*s^2-2*r+2*s, l*s^2+r*s^2-2*l*s+2*r*s-3*s^2-4*l-6*s-4, l*r-1/2*l*s+1/2*r*s-l-1/2*s-1, 
  1/2*l*s+1/2*r*s+k-l-3/2*s-1 ]
[ [ 2, 9 ], [ 3, 8 ], [ 4, 5, 7 ], [ 6 ] ]  # Rank is 5 but there are at least 7 distinct rows even if we assume that the row equality is feasible#

2=7 [ l*r^2-l*r*s+l*r-2*l*s-r^2-l-2*r-1, l*r-l*s+k-r ]
2=9 [ l*r+s^2+l-r+3*s+1, k*s^2+l*s^2+3*k*s+2*l*s+2*k+l+s+1, k*r-s^2+k+r-2*s ]
3=4 [ l*r*s-l*s^2+2*l*r-l*s+s^2+l+2*s+1, -l*r+l*s+k-s ]
3=5 [ l*s+r^2+l+3*r-s+1, k*s-r^2+k-2*r+s, k*r^2+l*r^2+3*k*r+2*l*r+2*k+l+r+1 ]
[ [ 2, 9 ], [ 3, 6 ], [ 4, 5, 7, 8 ] ]# Rank is 4 but there are at least 5 distinct rows even if we assume that the row equality is feasible#

2=7 [ l*r^2-l*r*s+l*r-2*l*s-r^2-r, l*r-l*s+k-r ]
2=9 [ l*r+s^2+l-r+3*s+1, k*s^2+l*s^2+3*k*s+l*s-s^2+2*k-s, k*r-s^2+k-s ]
3=4 [ l*r*s-l*s^2+2*l*r-l*s+s^2+s, -l*r+l*s+k-s ]
3=8 [ l*s+r*s+l+2*r+1, k*s-r*s+k-s, k*r-l*r-2*r^2+k-l-3*r-1 ]
4=8 [ l*r+r*s+s, k-l-2*r-1 ]
5=7 [ l*s+r^2+r, k-l-2*r-1 ]
[ [ 2, 9 ], [ 3, 4, 5, 7, 8 ], [ 6 ] ] # Rank is 4 but there are at least 5 distinct rows even if we assume that the row equality is feasible#

2=7 [ r^2*s-3/2*r*s^2+1/2*s^3, l*s+2*r*s-s^2+s, l*r^2+2*r*s^2-s^3-r^2+3*r*s-s^2, l*r+2*r*s-s^2+k-r+s ]
